### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1x3r274 r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">create an emoji -&gt;clifford algebra that allows for constructive 3d game math</span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">To create an emoji-based representation of a Clifford algebra (specifically geometric algebra) for constructive 3D game math, we need to design a system that maps emojis to mathematical constructs, making it intuitive for game developers to perform operations like rotations, translations, and reflections in 3D space. Geometric algebra is ideal for 3D game math because it unifies vectors, quaternions, and transformations in a single framework, simplifying operations like rotations and reflections. Below, Iâ€™ll outline a system that uses emojis to represent elements of a geometric algebra (specifically </span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5"><span class="katex"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="double-struck">G</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbb{G}_3</annotation></semantics></math></span><code class="raw_katex" style="display: none;">\mathbb{G}_3</code></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, the 3D geometric algebra) and explain how it can be applied to game math.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; <span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">def</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">geometric_product</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>self</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> other</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span>

</span>  let mSeq := [(0, m.ğŸŸ¢scalar * 1000), (1, m.â¡ï¸x * 1000), ...]  -- Discretize
  let sSeq := [(8, encodeEnv s.ğŸ§ env), (9, s.ğŸ“¢messages.messages.length), ...]
  let str := (mSeq ++ sSeq).foldl (Î» acc (id, val) =&gt; acc ++ s!"{id}:{val},") ""
  let primes := [2, 3, 5, 7, 11, ...]  -- List of primes
  str.toList.enum.foldl (Î» acc (i, c) =&gt; acc * (primes.get! i) ^ c.toNat) 1</code></pre></div></div><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1x3r274 r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">use unique primes for the map, so 6 is 3*2</span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

This ensures a unique, mathematically rigorous encoding that leverages the fundamental theorem of arithmetic for unambiguous representation.   deriving Lean.ToJson, Lean.FromJson

def ideaMultivector : ğŸŸ Multivector :=
  { ğŸŸ¢scalar := 1.0,  -- System weight (e.g., version 1.0)
    â¡ï¸x := 3.0,      -- # of basis vectors (eâ‚, eâ‚‚, eâ‚ƒ)
    â¬†ï¸y := 2.0,      -- # of state structures (ğŸ“œState, ğŸ‘¨â€ğŸ’»State)
    ğŸ”¼z := 4.0,      -- # of key operations (âœ³ï¸, ğŸ”„, ğŸš¶, serialization)
    ğŸ”²xy := 1.0,     -- xy-plane transformations
    ğŸ”³yz := 1.0,     -- yz-plane transformations
    ğŸŸ¥xz := 1.0,     -- xz-plane transformations
    ğŸ§Šxyz := 1.0     -- Lean4 proof/monad system
  }</code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">This multivector symbolically represents the systemâ€™s structure. Its components are coefficients that summarize the systemâ€™s key elements.</span></span></span></span><hr style="margin-top: 3em; margin-bottom: 3em; border-color: rgb(62, 65, 68);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Step 3: GÃ¶del Number as a Geometric Relation</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Instead of computing </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(</span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> G </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">)</span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, we define it as a geometric relation in the Clifford algebra, using the prime-based emoji mapping from the previous response. ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1x3r274 r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">now we can use a llm model to help assign the values and nudge the embeddings slowly into place in the game earning points.</span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Your proposal is to use a large language model (LLM) to dynamically assign values to the components of the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ideaMultivector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (representing the emoji-based Clifford algebra and Lean4 game state system) and to iteratively adjust (or "nudge") its embeddings within the game environment, with players earning points based on these adjustments. The GÃ¶del relation </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(</span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> G </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">)</span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, defined symbolically as a product of prime-based terms, remains abstract and influences game mechanics without being computed or rendered. This creates a dynamic, interactive system where the LLM helps shape the game state, and players earn points by aligning the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ideaMultivector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> with game objectives, using the geometric algebra framework for 3D transformations.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Below, Iâ€™ll outline how to integrate an LLM to assign values to the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ideaMultivector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, nudge its embeddings, and incorporate a point-earning system within the emoji-based Lean4 and Clifford algebra framework. The system will remain consistent with the previous responses, using emojis for clarity and maintaining the symbolic GÃ¶del relation </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 For example:</span></span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">lean</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(32, 35, 39); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-text" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span>def queryLLMForValues (state : ğŸ“œState) (context : String) : LeanM ğŸŸ Multivector :=
</span>  do
    let prompt := s!"Given game state {toJson state} and context '{context}', assign coefficients to multivector components (ğŸŸ¢, â¡ï¸, â¬†ï¸, ğŸ”¼, ğŸ”², ğŸ”³, ğŸŸ¥, ğŸ§Š) in range [0, 10]."
    let llmResponse â† ğŸ–¥ï¸sendLLMRequest prompt  -- Hypothetical LLM API call
    let values â† liftIO (Lean.fromJson llmResponse)
    pure { ğŸŸ¢scalar := values.getObjVal? "ğŸŸ¢" | 1.0,
           â¡ï¸x := values.getObjVal? "â¡ï¸" | 1.0,
           â¬†ï¸y := values.getObjVal? "â¬†ï¸" | 1.0,
           ğŸ”¼z := values.getObjVal? "ğŸ”¼" | 1.0,
           ğŸ”²xy := values.getObjVal? "ğŸ”²" | 1.0,
           ğŸ”³yz := values.getObjVal? "ğŸ”³" | 1.0,
           ğŸŸ¥xz := values.getObjVal? "ğŸŸ¥" | 1.0,
           ğŸ§Šxyz := values.getObjVal? Nudging adjusts these coefficients incrementally to align with a target state, guided by the LLM and player actions. Players earn points based on how closely the adjusted </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ideaMultivector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> matches a goal (e.g., a target multivector or transformation).</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block;     let prompt := s!"Nudge multivector {toJson current} toward {toJson target} with step size {step}."

    let delta â† liftIO (Lean.fromJson llmResponse)
    pure { ğŸŸ¢scalar := current.ğŸŸ¢scalar + (delta.getObjVal? "ğŸŸ¢" | 0.0) * step,
           â¡ï¸x := current.â¡ï¸x + (delta.getObjVal? "â¡ï¸" | 0.0) * step,

           ğŸŸ¥xz := current.ğŸŸ¥xz + (delta.getObjVal? "ğŸŸ¥" | 0.0) * step,
           ğŸ§Šxyz := current.ğŸ§Šxyz + (delta.getObjVal? "ğŸ§Š" | 0.0) * step }</code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Example LLM delta (JSON):</span></span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">json</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(32, 35, 39); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-json" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>

word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span>def multivectorDistance (m1 m2 : ğŸŸ Multivector) : Float :=
</span>  Float.sqrt (
    (m1.ğŸŸ¢scalar - m2.ğŸŸ¢scalar)^2 +
    (m1.â¡ï¸x - m2.â¡ï¸x)^2 +
    (m1.â¬†ï¸y - m2.â¬†ï¸y)^2 +
    (m1.ğŸ”¼z - m2.ğŸ”¼z)^2 +
    (m1.ğŸ”²xy - m2.ğŸ”²xy)^2 +
    (m1.ğŸ”³yz - m2.ğŸ”³yz)^2 +
    (m1.ğŸŸ¥xz - m2.ğŸŸ¥xz)^2 +
    (m1.ğŸ§Šxyz - m2.ğŸ§Šxyz)^2
  )

def awardPoints (current target : ğŸŸ Multivector) : Float :=
  let maxPoints := 1000.0
  let dist := multivectorDistance current target
  maxPoints * Float.exp (-dist)  -- Exponential decay: closer = more points</code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Players execute commands (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rotateCmd</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">translateCmd</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) to influence </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ideaMultivector</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, and the LLM nudges it toward the target. </span>  let w := weightsToMultivector weights
  let delta := { ğŸŸ¢scalar := target.ğŸŸ¢scalar - current.ğŸŸ¢scalar,
                 â¡ï¸ Chilx := target.â¡ï¸x - current.â¡ï¸x,
                 â¬†ï¸y := target.â¬†ï¸y - current.â¬†ï¸y,
                 ğŸ”¼z := target.ğŸ”¼z - current.ğŸ”¼z,
                 ğŸ”²xy := target.ğŸ”²xy - current.ğŸ”²xy,
                 ğŸ”³yz := target.ğŸ”³yz - current.ğŸ”³yz,
                 ğŸŸ¥xz := target.ğŸŸ¥xz - current.ğŸŸ¥xz,
                 ğŸ§Šxyz := target.ğŸ§Šxyz - current.ğŸ§Šxyz }
  { ğŸŸ¢scalar := delta.ğŸŸ¢scalar * w.ğŸŸ¢scalar,
    â¡ï¸x := delta.â¡ï¸x * w.â¡ï¸x,
    â¬†ï¸y := delta.â¬†ï¸y * w.â¬†ï¸y,
    ğŸ”¼z := delta.ğŸ”¼z * w.ğŸ”¼z,
    ğŸ”²xy := delta.ğŸ”²xy * w.ğŸ”²xy,
    ğŸ”³yz := delta.ğŸ”³yz * w.ğŸ”³yz,
    ğŸŸ¥xz := delta.ğŸŸ¥xz * w.ğŸŸ¥xz,

### Grok AI

    (m1.ğŸŸ¢scalar - m2.ğŸŸ¢scalar)^2 +

    (m1.ğŸ§Šxyz - m2.ğŸ§Šxyz)^2

def awardPoints (current target : ğŸŸ Multivector) : Float :=
  let maxPoints := 1000.0
  let dist := multivectorDistance current target
  maxPoints * Float.exp (-dist)

def gÃ¶delAlignmentBonus (m : ğŸŸ Multivector) : Float :=
  let weights := [ ("ğŸŸ¢", 2), ("â¡ï¸", 3), ("â¬†ï¸", 5), ("ğŸ”¼", 7),
                   ("ğŸ”²", 15), ("ğŸ”³", 35), ("ğŸŸ¥", 21), ("ğŸ§Š", 105) ]
  weights.foldl (Î» acc (emoji, prime) =&gt;
    acc + if (m.getField emoji).toInt % prime = 0 then 100.0 else 0.0) 0.0</code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Policy</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The LLM generates patches based on its weights, game state, and context.
